					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT

						}
					}				
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					k_iron_isles = {

					}
				}
				k_westerlands = {

							years = 5
						}

							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}

						}

			}

					}

						who = ROOT
						years = 100
					}

						join_attacker_wars = PREV
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

3015276 = {
	name="Джеффрой"	# a lord, at the time of the Dance of Dragons
	dynasty=276

	religion="the_seven"
	culture="reachman"

	father=3011276
	mother=4011276

	8114.1.1 = {birth="8114.1.1"}
	8129.4.1={ #Dance of the Dragons
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.1.1 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}				
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1 = {	#Hightower host enforced his submission
		add_trait=knight 
		add_trait=skilled_warrior
		effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = supporting_king
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}				
					set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 6 } #reach
				}
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_loyal_to_crown
							years = 5
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_with_king
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_defender_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8136.1.1 = {add_spouse=27152} # Tilly Ryger
	8146.1.1 = {death = {death_reason = death_accident}}
}

			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.1.1 } }
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				set_character_flag = against_king
				clr_character_flag = neutral
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { 
						OR = {
							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}

				}
				e_iron_throne = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_joined_rebellion
							who = ROOT
							years = 20
						}
					}
				}
				c_dragonstone = {
					holder_scope = { 
						opinion = {
							who = ROOT
							modifier = opinion_joined_cause
						}
						reverse_opinion = {
							modifier = opinion_with_rebel_leader
							who = ROOT
							years = 100
						}
						ROOT = {
							join_attacker_wars = PREV
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	8130.1.1 = {	#Hightower host enforced his submission

			if = { 
				limit = { NOT = { start_date = 8130.10.22 } }

							tier = COUNT
							tier = DUKE
